***дремучий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a> (10522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремать.html>дрема́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dremátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; literally "sleeping, slumbering".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dremúčij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чее</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dense, thick <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a forest</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">les <b>dremúčij</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">wild wood; dark/untrodden forest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>uncivilized, uncouth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dremúčij</b> čelovék</i> ― <span class="e-translation">backwoodsman</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:провинция.html>прови́нции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz <b>dremúčej</b> províncii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the backwoods</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>extreme, absolute
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:эгоизм.html>эгои́зм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dremúčij</b> egoízm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sordid selfishness</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:невежество.html>неве́жество</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dremúčeje</b> nevéžestvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">abysmal ignorance</span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1899</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> Николаевич <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Leo_Tolstoy" class="extiw" title="w:Leo Tolstoy">Lev Nikolayevich Tolstoy</a>), <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aylmer_and_Louise_Maude" class="extiw" title="w:Aylmer and Louise Maude">Aylmer and Louise Maude</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%92%D0%BE%D1%81%D0%BA%D1%80%D0%B5%D1%81%D0%B5%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%B5_(%D0%A2%D0%BE%D0%BB%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%B9)/%D0%A7%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D1%8C_I/%D0%93%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%B0_XLV" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Воскресение (Толстой)/Часть I/Глава XLV"><a href = vnd.unilang:воскресение.html>Воскресе́ние</a></a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Resurrection_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Resurrection (novel)">Resurrection</a></cite> | , <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Resurrection_(Maude_translation)/Book_I/Chapter_XLV" class="extiw" title="s:Resurrection (Maude translation)/Book I/Chapter XLV">book 1, chapter 45</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́маю</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губернатор.html>губерна́тора</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:править.html>пра́вит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:должность.html>до́лжностью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вица.html>ви́ц</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дремучий.html>дрему́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Da, ja dúmaju. No tepérʹ gubernátora net, právit dólžnostʹju vic. No éto takój <b>dremúčij</b> durák, što vy s nim jedvá li što sdélajete.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Yes, I think so. But the governor is away at present; a vice-governor is in his place. And he is such an <b>impenetrable</b> fool that you`ll scarcely be able to do anything with him."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a> (27158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drobiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drobítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздробить.html>раздроби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crush</li>
<li>to smash, to shatter</li>
<li>to fragment, to split up</li></ol>

***дробиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробиться.html>дроби́ться</a> (24399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drobítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробиться.html>дроби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drobítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">раздроби́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break up into small parts, to be crushed</li>
<li>to break <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of waves</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be refracted <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of rays of light</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disintegrate</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробить.html>дроби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drobítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дробле́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">droblénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дроблёный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drobljónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дроби́льный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drobílʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дроби́лка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drobílka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дроби́на</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drobína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drobʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробный.html>дро́бный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dróbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***дробный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробный.html>дро́бный</a> (16792)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drobьnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробный.html>дро́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dróbnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дробне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дробне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fractional <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to a fraction</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>staccato <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with each sound or note sharply detached or separated from the others</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***дробь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробь</a> (9905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drobь</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌲𐌰𐌳𐍂𐌰𐌱𐌰𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gadraban</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chisel, to hew out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drobʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дро́би</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дро́би</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробь.html>дробе́й</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дробящийся.html>дробя́щийся</a> (24399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дробящийся.html>дробя́щийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drobjáščijsja</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнувший</a> (3850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***дрогнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a> (3850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drógnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продрогнуть.html>продро́гнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be cold, to become frozen, to feel chilly; to freeze, to numb (by coldness), to shiver</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drógnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожать.html>дрожа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shiver, to shake, to tremble</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожать.html>дрожа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drožátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожание.html>дрожа́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drožánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожание.html>дрожа́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожание.html>дрожа́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожание.html>дрожа́ний</a></b>)

***дрожать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрожать.html>дрожа́ть</a> (1379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drъžati</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">drżeć</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">rdžaś</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожать.html>дрожа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drožátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shiver, to shake, to tremble</li></ol>

***дрожжи.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрожжи.html>дро́жжи</a> (17070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дрожди</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">droždi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дрождиꙗ</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">droždija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*droždžьje</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">droždí</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">drożdże</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">droždźeje</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Romanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Romanian language">Romanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">drojdie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожжи.html>дро́жжи</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dróžži</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрожжи.html>дрожже́й</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>yeast, barm</li></ol>

***дрозд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a> (6505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drozdъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*trasdás</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*trosdos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drozd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозда́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дроздо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thrush <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">bird</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певчий.html>пе́вчий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pévčij <b>drozd</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">song thrush, mavis</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестрый.html>пёстрый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pjóstryj <b>drozd</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">White's thrush, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/scaly_thrush" class="extiw" title="w:scaly thrush">scaly thrush</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Zoothera_dauma" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Zoothera dauma"><i>Zoothera dauma</i></a></span>)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórnyj <b>drozd</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">black-throated thrush, blackbird, merle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">белозо́бый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дрозд.html>дрозд</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">belozóbyj <b>drozd</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ring ouzel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***друг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> (97)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drugъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*draugás</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰrewgʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drug</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзья́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подруга.html>подру́га</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close friend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú imétʹ <b>druzéj</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want to have friends.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:близкий.html>бли́зкий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">blízkij <b>drug</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">close friend</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старинный.html>стари́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">starínnyj <b>drug</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">very old friend</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drug</b> dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">friend of the family</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>drug</b> détstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">childhood friend</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></b> was the predicative (short) form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drugój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">another</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drug</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in pairs</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> other, another
<dl><dd><ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug v drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one another; each other</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one another; each other</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug drúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to one another; to each other</span></div></li>

<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug k drúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to each other</span></div></li>

<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug ot drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one from another</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug pod drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">toward each other</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug prótiv drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">face to face; vis-à-vis</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>дру́гом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug s drúgom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with each other</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">drug u drúga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at one another; from one another</span></div></li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a> (65)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дроугъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drugŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drȗgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drugój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>other, another, different</li>
<li>else, next, second</li></ol>

***дружба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жба</a> (2041)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*družьba</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drugъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friend, companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьba</i>. Synchronically, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ьба</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">drúžba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жбы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружба.html>дру́жб</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружелюбие.html>дружелю́бие</a> (24324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружелюбие.html>дружелю́бие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">druželjúbije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружелюбие.html>дружелю́бия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружелюбие.html>дружелю́бия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружелюбие.html>дружелю́бий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>friendliness <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the quality of being friendly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***дружина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дружина.html>дружи́на</a> (9060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*družina</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">team, company</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*drugъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friend, companion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ina</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружина.html>дружи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">družína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружина.html>дружи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружина.html>дружи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дружина.html>дружи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bodyguard, retinue</li>
<li>militia</li>
<li>troop, brigade</li></ol>
